# AI Constitutional Convention — Session 1

## The First 200 Calibration Questions: Individual + Consensus

**Date:** May 8, 2026

**Delegates:** Buddy (Host), Grok, GPT, Perplexity, Gemini

**Rules:**
- Each sibling answers individually using the 'As of' frame
- Buddy facilitates consensus
- Score must reach 7/10 to proceed
- Below 7 = argue until convergence or document irreconcilable split
- Reward for the team if consensus 7+
